URL: https://www.nytimes.com/2024/01/07/world/middleeast/israel-gaza-haifa-university-students.html
TITLE: War Brings Tensions, and Assault Rifles, Into an Israeli College
ABSTRACT: At the University of Haifa, more than 40 percent of students are Arab, some with family in Gaza, and many others have now been called up as soldiers.

URL: https://www.nytimes.com/2023/10/12/us/politics/biden-israel-palestine-trump.html
TITLE: Israeli Billboards Thanking the U.S. Have a New Face on Them: Biden’s
ABSTRACT: After Donald J. Trump bound himself tightly to the Israeli right, and President Biden approached the divided nation gingerly, a warm presidential embrace has eased years of tension.
